 In North India, as the temperature continues to fall, the mixing height is coming down
 mixing hit vaataavaran main vah oonchai hoti he jahaan par jameen par ho rahaa pradooshan visarjeet hota he
 The mixing height in North India is up to 4 km during the summer, but it falls below 1 km during the winter season
 mixing hit ghatane se vaataavaran main maujuud vaayu pradooshan ghanaa ho jaataa he
 It also takes time for its removal, at this time, the night temperature in all areas of North India, including Delhi NCR, is around 16 degrees Celsius and the day temperature is around 32 degrees
 mausam vibhaag kaa anumaan he ki in 4 dinon main isamen or giravat aa sakati he
 In this case, the mixing height will decrease and the air pollution in the atmosphere will become dense and pungent
 dilli or aasapaas ke ilaakon main pradooshan ke ghanatv main badhotaree dekhi ja rahi he
 According to the data being recorded under the Safar Program of the Meteorological Department, at this time the wind blowing in all the areas of Delhi NCR has become very bad
 air quality index ke mutabik isko veri pur category main rakhaa gaya he
 It will remain in the same category of Very Poor in the next 24 hours, but after that, on October 30, its condition is expected to worsen on the day of Diwali

 According to Vijay Kumar Soni, this time the pollution due to fire in the residue left after harvesting the paddy crop in Punjab, Haryana and Uttar Pradesh has also been less than in previous years

 5 veri pur category main hai
 Their condition is likely to be serious on Deepawali

 is vajah se bharatiyon ke liye ye nav varsh bahut mahatvapurn hota he

 desanvi ko kai kitabon ke liye janaa jaataa he
 He is credited with several books, in which he is known for his work on Maulana Abul Kalam, Mirza Ghalib and Allama Mohammad Iqbal
 aaj se 87 saal pehle desanvi kaa janm bihar ke desna gaanv main urdu ke professor mohammad said raja ke yahaan hua tha

 Xavier's and after that he joined Safia Post Graduate College in 1961 as a professor
